  1760	func (am *DefaultAccountManager) GetOrCreateAccountByPrivateDomain(ctx context.Context, initiatorId, domain string) (*types.Account, bool, error) {
  1761	        cancel := am.Store.AcquireGlobalLock(ctx)
  1762	        defer cancel()
  1763	
  1764	        existingPrimaryAccountID, err := am.Store.GetAccountIDByPrivateDomain(ctx, store.LockingStrengthShare, domain)
  1765	        if handleNotFound(err) != nil {
  1766	                return nil, false, err
  1767	        }
  1768	
  1769	        // a primary account already exists for this private domain
  1770	        if err == nil {
  1771	                existingAccount, err := am.Store.GetAccount(ctx, existingPrimaryAccountID)
  1772	                if err != nil {
  1773	                        return nil, false, err
  1774	                }
  1775	
  1776	                return existingAccount, false, nil
  1777	        }
  1778	
  1779	        // create a new account for this private domain
  1780	        // retry twice for new ID clashes
  1781	        for range 2 {
  1782	                accountId := xid.New().String()
  1783	
  1784	                exists, err := am.Store.AccountExists(ctx, store.LockingStrengthShare, accountId)
  1785	                if err != nil || exists {
  1786	                        continue
  1787	                }
  1788	
  1789	                network := types.NewNetwork()
  1790	                peers := make(map[string]*nbpeer.Peer)
  1791	                users := make(map[string]*types.User)
  1792	                routes := make(map[route.ID]*route.Route)
  1793	                setupKeys := map[string]*types.SetupKey{}
  1794	                nameServersGroups := make(map[string]*nbdns.NameServerGroup)
  1795	
  1796	                dnsSettings := types.DNSSettings{
  1797	                        DisabledManagementGroups: make([]string, 0),
  1798	                }
  1799	
  1800	                newAccount := &types.Account{
  1801	                        Id:        accountId,
  1802	                        CreatedAt: time.Now().UTC(),
  1803	                        SetupKeys: setupKeys,
  1804	                        Network:   network,
  1805	                        Peers:     peers,
  1806	                        Users:     users,

  1829	                }

  1837	                }
  1838

  1841	        }
  1842	
  1843	        return nil, false, status.Errorf(status.Internal, "failed to get or create new account by private domain")
  1844	}

    63	// ManagementLegacyPort is the port that was used before by the Management gRPC server.
    64	// It is used for backward compatibility now.
    65	const ManagementLegacyPort = 33073
    66	
    67	var (
    68	        mgmtPort                int
    69	        mgmtMetricsPort         int
    70	        mgmtLetsencryptDomain   string
    71	        mgmtSingleAccModeDomain string
    72	        certFile                string
    73	        certKey                 string
    74	        config                  *types.Config
    75	
    76	        kaep = keepalive.EnforcementPolicy{
    77	                MinTime:             15 * time.Second,
    78	                PermitWithoutStream: true,
    79	        }
    80	
    81	        kasp = keepalive.ServerParameters{
    82	                MaxConnectionIdle:     15 * time.Second,
    83	                MaxConnectionAgeGrace: 5 * time.Second,
    84	                Time:                  5 * time.Second,
    85	                Timeout:               2 * time.Second,
    86	        }
    87	
    88	        mgmtCmd = &cobra.Command{
    89	                Use:   "management",
    90	                Short: "start NetBird Management Server",
    91	                PreRunE: func(cmd *cobra.Command, args []string) error {
    92	                        flag.Parse()
    93	
    94	                        //nolint
    95	                        ctx := context.WithValue(cmd.Context(), hook.ExecutionContextKey, hook.SystemSource)
    96	
    97	                        err := util.InitLog(logLevel, logFile)
    98	                        if err != nil {
    99	                                return fmt.Errorf("failed initializing log %v", err)
   100	                        }
   101	
   102	                        // detect whether user specified a port
   103	                        userPort := cmd.Flag("port").Changed
   104	
   105	                        config, err = loadMgmtConfig(ctx, types.MgmtConfigPath)
   106	                        if err != nil {
   107	                                return fmt.Errorf("failed reading provided config file: %s: %v", types.MgmtConfigPath, err)
   108	                        }
   109	
   110	                        if cmd.Flag(idpSignKeyRefreshEnabledFlagName).Changed {
   111	                                config.HttpConfig.IdpSignKeyRefreshEnabled = idpSignKeyRefreshEnabled
   112	                        }
   113	
   114	                        tlsEnabled := false
   115	                        if mgmtLetsencryptDomain != "" || (config.HttpConfig.CertFile != "" && config.HttpConfig.CertKey != "") {
   116	                                tlsEnabled = true
   117	                        }
   118	
   119	                        if !userPort {
   120	                                // different defaults for port when tls enabled/disabled
   121	                                if tlsEnabled {
   122	                                        mgmtPort = 443
   123	                                } else {
   124	                                        mgmtPort = 80
   125	                                }
   126	                        }
   127	
   128	                        _, valid := dns.IsDomainName(dnsDomain)
   129	                        if !valid || len(dnsDomain) > 192 {
   130	                                return fmt.Errorf("failed parsing the provided dns-domain. Valid status: %t, Length: %d", valid, len(dnsDomain))
   131	                        }
   132	
   133	                        return nil
   134	                },
   135	                RunE: func(cmd *cobra.Command, args []string) error {
   136	                        flag.Parse()
   137	
   138	                        ctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(cmd.Context())
   139	                        defer cancel()
   140	                        //nolint
   141	                        ctx = context.WithValue(ctx, hook.ExecutionContextKey, hook.SystemSource)
   142	
   143	                        err := handleRebrand(cmd)
   144	                        if err != nil {
   145	                                return fmt.Errorf("failed to migrate files %v", err)
   146	                        }
   147	
   148	                        if _, err = os.Stat(config.Datadir); os.IsNotExist(err) {
   149	                                err = os.MkdirAll(config.Datadir, 0755)
   150	                                if err != nil {
   151	                                        return fmt.Errorf("failed creating datadir: %s: %v", config.Datadir, err)
   152	                                }
   153	                        }
   154	                        appMetrics, err := telemetry.NewDefaultAppMetrics(cmd.Context())
   155	                        if err != nil {
   156	                                return err
   157	                        }
   158	                        err = appMetrics.Expose(ctx, mgmtMetricsPort, "/metrics")
   159	                        if err != nil {
   160	                                return err
   161	                        }
   162	
   163	                        integrationMetrics, err := integrations.InitIntegrationMetrics(ctx, appMetrics)
   164	                        if err != nil {
   165	                                return err
   166	                        }
   167	
   168	                        store, err := store.NewStore(ctx, config.StoreConfig.Engine, config.Datadir, appMetrics, false)
   169	                        if err != nil {
   170	                                return fmt.Errorf("failed creating Store: %s: %v", config.Datadir, err)
   171	                        }
   172	                        peersUpdateManager := server.NewPeersUpdateManager(appMetrics)
   173	
   174	                        var idpManager idp.Manager
   175	                        if config.IdpManagerConfig != nil {
   176	                                idpManager, err = idp.NewManager(ctx, *config.IdpManagerConfig, appMetrics)
   177	                                if err != nil {
   178	                                        return fmt.Errorf("failed retrieving a new idp manager with err: %v", err)
   179	                                }
   180	                        }
   181	
   182	                        if disableSingleAccMode {
   183	                                mgmtSingleAccModeDomain = ""
   184	                        }
   185	                        eventStore, key, err := integrations.InitEventStore(ctx, config.Datadir, config.DataStoreEncryptionKey, integrationMetrics)
   186	                        if err != nil {
   187	                                return fmt.Errorf("failed to initialize database: %s", err)
   188	                        }
   189	
   190	                        if config.DataStoreEncryptionKey != key {
   191	                                log.WithContext(ctx).Infof("update config with activity store key")
   192	                                config.DataStoreEncryptionKey = key
   193	                                err := updateMgmtConfig(ctx, types.MgmtConfigPath, config)
   194	                                if err != nil {
   195	                                        return fmt.Errorf("failed to write out store encryption key: %s", err)
   196	                                }
   197	                        }
   198	
   199	                        geo, err := geolocation.NewGeolocation(ctx, config.Datadir, !disableGeoliteUpdate)
   200	                        if err != nil {
   201	                                log.WithContext(ctx).Warnf("could not initialize geolocation service. proceeding without geolocation support: %v", err)
   202	                        } else {
   203	                                log.WithContext(ctx).Infof("geolocation service has been initialized from %s", config.Datadir)
   204	                        }
   205	
   206	                        integratedPeerValidator, err := integrations.NewIntegratedValidator(ctx, eventStore)
   207	                        if err != nil {
   208	                                return fmt.Errorf("failed to initialize integrated peer validator: %v", err)
   209	                        }
   210	
   211	                        permissionsManager := integrations.InitPermissionsManager(store)
   212	                        userManager := users.NewManager(store)
   213	                        extraSettingsManager := integrations.NewManager(eventStore)
   214	                        settingsManager := settings.NewManager(store, userManager, extraSettingsManager, permissionsManager)
   215	                        peersManager := peers.NewManager(store, permissionsManager)
   216	                        proxyController := integrations.NewController(store)
   217	                        accountManager, err := server.BuildManager(ctx, store, peersUpdateManager, idpManager, mgmtSingleAccModeDomain,
   218	                                dnsDomain, eventStore, geo, userDeleteFromIDPEnabled, integratedPeerValidator, appMetrics, proxyController, settingsManager, permissionsManager)
   219	                        if err != nil {
   220	                                return fmt.Errorf("failed to build default manager: %v", err)
   221	                        }
   222	
   223	                        secretsManager := server.NewTimeBasedAuthSecretsManager(peersUpdateManager, config.TURNConfig, config.Relay, settingsManager)
   224	
   225	                        trustedPeers := config.ReverseProxy.TrustedPeers
   226	                        defaultTrustedPeers := []netip.Prefix{netip.MustParsePrefix("0.0.0.0/0"), netip.MustParsePrefix("::/0")}
   227	                        if len(trustedPeers) == 0 || slices.Equal[[]netip.Prefix](trustedPeers, defaultTrustedPeers) {
   228	                                log.WithContext(ctx).Warn("TrustedPeers are configured to default value '0.0.0.0/0', '::/0'. This allows connection IP spoofing.")
   229	                                trustedPeers = defaultTrustedPeers
   230	                        }
   231	                        trustedHTTPProxies := config.ReverseProxy.TrustedHTTPProxies
   232	                        trustedProxiesCount := config.ReverseProxy.TrustedHTTPProxiesCount
   233	                        if len(trustedHTTPProxies) > 0 && trustedProxiesCount > 0 {
   234	                                log.WithContext(ctx).Warn("TrustedHTTPProxies and TrustedHTTPProxiesCount both are configured. " +
   235	                                        "This is not recommended way to extract X-Forwarded-For. Consider using one of these options.")
   236	                        }
   237	                        realipOpts := []realip.Option{
   238	                                realip.WithTrustedPeers(trustedPeers),
   239	                                realip.WithTrustedProxies(trustedHTTPProxies),
   240	                                realip.WithTrustedProxiesCount(trustedProxiesCount),
   241	                                realip.WithHeaders([]string{realip.XForwardedFor, realip.XRealIp}),
   242	                        }
   243	                        gRPCOpts := []grpc.ServerOption{
   244	                                grpc.KeepaliveEnforcementPolicy(kaep),
   245	                                grpc.KeepaliveParams(kasp),
   246	                                grpc.ChainUnaryInterceptor(realip.UnaryServerInterceptorOpts(realipOpts...), unaryInterceptor),
   247	                                grpc.ChainStreamInterceptor(realip.StreamServerInterceptorOpts(realipOpts...), streamInterceptor),
   248	                        }
   249	
   250	                        var certManager *autocert.Manager
   251	                        var tlsConfig *tls.Config
   252	                        tlsEnabled := false
   253	                        if config.HttpConfig.LetsEncryptDomain != "" {
   254	                                certManager, err = encryption.CreateCertManager(config.Datadir, config.HttpConfig.LetsEncryptDomain)
   255	                                if err != nil {
   256	                                        return fmt.Errorf("failed creating LetsEncrypt cert manager: %v", err)
   257	                                }
   258	                                transportCredentials := credentials.NewTLS(certManager.TLSConfig())
   259	                                gRPCOpts = append(gRPCOpts, grpc.Creds(transportCredentials))
   260	                                tlsEnabled = true
   261	                        } else if config.HttpConfig.CertFile != "" && config.HttpConfig.CertKey != "" {
   262	                                tlsConfig, err = loadTLSConfig(config.HttpConfig.CertFile, config.HttpConfig.CertKey)
   263	                                if err != nil {
   264	                                        log.WithContext(ctx).Errorf("cannot load TLS credentials: %v", err)
   265	                                        return err
   266	                                }
   267	                                transportCredentials := credentials.NewTLS(tlsConfig)
   268	                                gRPCOpts = append(gRPCOpts, grpc.Creds(transportCredentials))
   269	                                tlsEnabled = true
   270	                        }
   271	
   272	                        authManager := auth.NewManager(store,
   273	                                config.HttpConfig.AuthIssuer,
   274	                                config.HttpConfig.AuthAudience,
   275	                                config.HttpConfig.AuthKeysLocation,
   276	                                config.HttpConfig.AuthUserIDClaim,
   277	                                config.GetAuthAudiences(),
   278	                                config.HttpConfig.IdpSignKeyRefreshEnabled)
   279	
   280	                        groupsManager := groups.NewManager(store, permissionsManager, accountManager)
   281	                        resourcesManager := resources.NewManager(store, permissionsManager, groupsManager, accountManager)
   282	                        routersManager := routers.NewManager(store, permissionsManager, accountManager)
   283	                        networksManager := networks.NewManager(store, permissionsManager, resourcesManager, routersManager, accountManager)
   284	
   285	                        httpAPIHandler, err := nbhttp.NewAPIHandler(ctx, accountManager, networksManager, resourcesManager, routersManager, groupsManager, geo, authManager, appMetrics, integratedPeerValidator, proxyController, permissionsManager, peersManager, settingsManager)
   286	
   287	                        if err != nil {
   288	                                return fmt.Errorf("failed creating HTTP API handler: %v", err)
   289	                        }
   290	
   291	                        ephemeralManager := server.NewEphemeralManager(store, accountManager)
   292	                        ephemeralManager.LoadInitialPeers(ctx)
   293	
   294	                        gRPCAPIHandler := grpc.NewServer(gRPCOpts...)
   295	                        srv, err := server.NewServer(ctx, config, accountManager, settingsManager, peersUpdateManager, secretsManager, appMetrics, ephemeralManager, authManager)
   296	                        if err != nil {
   297	                                return fmt.Errorf("failed creating gRPC API handler: %v", err)
   298	                        }
   299	                        mgmtProto.RegisterManagementServiceServer(gRPCAPIHandler, srv)
   300	
   301	                        installationID, err := getInstallationID(ctx, store)
   302	                        if err != nil {
   303	                                log.WithContext(ctx).Errorf("cannot load TLS credentials: %v", err)
   304	                                return err
   305	                        }
   306	
   307	                        if !disableMetrics {
   308	                                idpManager := "disabled"
   309	                                if config.IdpManagerConfig != nil && config.IdpManagerConfig.ManagerType != "" {
   310	                                        idpManager = config.IdpManagerConfig.ManagerType
   311	                                }
   312	                                metricsWorker := metrics.NewWorker(ctx, installationID, store, peersUpdateManager, idpManager)
   313	                                go metricsWorker.Run(ctx)
   314	                        }
   315	
   316	                        var compatListener net.Listener
   317	                        if mgmtPort != ManagementLegacyPort {
   318	                                // The Management gRPC server was running on port 33073 previously. Old agents that are already connected to it
   319	                                // are using port 33073. For compatibility purposes we keep running a 2nd gRPC server on port 33073.
   320	                                compatListener, err = serveGRPC(ctx, gRPCAPIHandler, ManagementLegacyPort)
   321	                                if err != nil {
   322	                                        return err
   323	                                }
   324	                                log.WithContext(ctx).Infof("running gRPC backward compatibility server: %s", compatListener.Addr().String())
   325	                        }
   326	
   327	                        rootHandler := handlerFunc(gRPCAPIHandler, httpAPIHandler)
   328	                        var listener net.Listener
   329	                        if certManager != nil {
   330	                                // a call to certManager.Listener() always creates a new listener so we do it once
   331	                                cml := certManager.Listener()
   332	                                if mgmtPort == 443 {
   333	                                        // CertManager, HTTP and gRPC API all on the same port
   334	                                        rootHandler = certManager.HTTPHandler(rootHandler)
   335	                                        listener = cml
   336	                                } else {
   337	                                        listener, err = tls.Listen("tcp", fmt.Sprintf(":%d", mgmtPort), certManager.TLSConfig())
   338	                                        if err != nil {
   339	                                                return fmt.Errorf("failed creating TLS listener on port %d: %v", mgmtPort, err)
   340	                                        }
   341	                                        log.WithContext(ctx).Infof("running HTTP server (LetsEncrypt challenge handler): %s", cml.Addr().String())
   342	                                        serveHTTP(ctx, cml, certManager.HTTPHandler(nil))
   343	                                }
   344	                        } else if tlsConfig != nil {
   345	                                listener, err = tls.Listen("tcp", fmt.Sprintf(":%d", mgmtPort), tlsConfig)
   346	                                if err != nil {
   347	                                        return fmt.Errorf("failed creating TLS listener on port %d: %v", mgmtPort, err)
   348	                                }
   349	                        } else {
   350	                                listener, err = net.Listen("tcp", fmt.Sprintf(":%d", mgmtPort))
   351	                                if err != nil {
   352	                                        return fmt.Errorf("failed creating TCP listener on port %d: %v", mgmtPort, err)
   353	                                }
   354	                        }
   355	
   356	                        log.WithContext(ctx).Infof("management server version %s", version.NetbirdVersion())
   357	                        log.WithContext(ctx).Infof("running HTTP server and gRPC server on the same port: %s", listener.Addr().String())
   358	                        serveGRPCWithHTTP(ctx, listener, rootHandler, tlsEnabled)
   359	
   360	                        SetupCloseHandler()
   361	
   362	                        <-stopCh
   363	                        integratedPeerValidator.Stop(ctx)
   364	                        if geo != nil {
   365	                                _ = geo.Stop()
   366	                        }
   367	                        ephemeralManager.Stop()
   368	                        _ = appMetrics.Close()
   369	                        _ = listener.Close()
   370	                        if certManager != nil {
   371	                                _ = certManager.Listener().Close()
   372	                        }
   373	                        gRPCAPIHandler.Stop()
   374	                        _ = store.Close(ctx)
   375	                        _ = eventStore.Close(ctx)
   376	                        log.WithContext(ctx).Infof("stopped Management Service")
   377	
   378	                        return nil
   379	                },
   380	        }
   381	)
   382	
   383	func unaryInterceptor(
   384	        ctx context.Context,
   385	        req interface{},
   386	        info *grpc.UnaryServerInfo,
   387	        handler grpc.UnaryHandler,
   388	) (interface{}, error) {
   389	        reqID := uuid.New().String()
   390	        //nolint
   391	        ctx = context.WithValue(ctx, hook.ExecutionContextKey, hook.GRPCSource)
   392	        //nolint
   393	        ctx = context.WithValue(ctx, nbContext.RequestIDKey, reqID)
   394	        return handler(ctx, req)
   395	}
   396	
   397	func streamInterceptor(
   398	        srv interface{},
   399	        ss grpc.ServerStream,
   400	        info *grpc.StreamServerInfo,
   401	        handler grpc.StreamHandler,
   402	) error {
   403	        reqID := uuid.New().String()
   404	        wrapped := grpcMiddleware.WrapServerStream(ss)
   405	        //nolint
   406	        ctx := context.WithValue(ss.Context(), hook.ExecutionContextKey, hook.GRPCSource)
   407	        //nolint
   408	        wrapped.WrappedContext = context.WithValue(ctx, nbContext.RequestIDKey, reqID)
   409	        return handler(srv, wrapped)
   410	}
   411	
   412	func notifyStop(ctx context.Context, msg string) {
   413	        select {
   414	        case stopCh <- 1:
   415	                log.WithContext(ctx).Error(msg)
   416	        default:
   417	                // stop has been already called, nothing to report
   418	        }
   419	}
   420	
   421	func getInstallationID(ctx context.Context, store store.Store) (string, error) {
   422	        installationID := store.GetInstallationID()
   423	        if installationID != "" {
   424	                return installationID, nil
   425	        }
   426	
   427	        installationID = strings.ToUpper(uuid.New().String())
   428	        err := store.SaveInstallationID(ctx, installationID)
   429	        if err != nil {
   430	                return "", err
   431	        }
   432	        return installationID, nil
   433	}
   434	
   435	func serveGRPC(ctx context.Context, grpcServer *grpc.Server, port int) (net.Listener, error) {
   436	        listener, err := net.Listen("tcp", fmt.Sprintf(":%d", port))
   437	        if err != nil {
   438	                return nil, err
   439	        }
   440	        go func() {
   441	                err := grpcServer.Serve(listener)
   442	                if err != nil {
   443	                        notifyStop(ctx, fmt.Sprintf("failed running gRPC server on port %d: %v", port, err))
   444	                }
   445	        }()
   446	        return listener, nil
   447	}
   448

   156	// BuildManager creates a new DefaultAccountManager with a provided Store
   157	func BuildManager(
   158	        ctx context.Context,
   159	        store store.Store,
   160	        peersUpdateManager *PeersUpdateManager,
   161	        idpManager idp.Manager,
   162	        singleAccountModeDomain string,
   163	        dnsDomain string,
   164	        eventStore activity.Store,
   165	        geo geolocation.Geolocation,
   166	        userDeleteFromIDPEnabled bool,
   167	        integratedPeerValidator integrated_validator.IntegratedValidator,
   168	        metrics telemetry.AppMetrics,
   169	        proxyController port_forwarding.Controller,
   170	        settingsManager settings.Manager,
   171	        permissionsManager permissions.Manager,
   172	) (*DefaultAccountManager, error) {
   173	        start := time.Now()
   174	        defer func() {
   175	                log.WithContext(ctx).Debugf("took %v to instantiate account manager", time.Since(start))
   176	        }()
   177	
   178	        am := &DefaultAccountManager{
   179	                Store:                    store,
   180	                geo:                      geo,
   181	                peersUpdateManager:       peersUpdateManager,
   182	                idpManager:               idpManager,
   183	                ctx:                      context.Background(),
   184	                cacheMux:                 sync.Mutex{},
   185	                cacheLoading:             map[string]chan struct{}{},
   186	                dnsDomain:                dnsDomain,
   187	                eventStore:               eventStore,
   188	                peerLoginExpiry:          NewDefaultScheduler(),
   189	                peerInactivityExpiry:     NewDefaultScheduler(),
   190	                userDeleteFromIDPEnabled: userDeleteFromIDPEnabled,
   191	                integratedPeerValidator:  integratedPeerValidator,
   192	                metrics:                  metrics,
   193	                requestBuffer:            NewAccountRequestBuffer(ctx, store),
   194	                proxyController:          proxyController,
   195	                settingsManager:          settingsManager,
   196	                permissionsManager:       permissionsManager,
   197	        }
   198	
   199	        am.startWarmup(ctx)
   200	
   201	        accountsCounter, err := store.GetAccountsCounter(ctx)
   202	        if err != nil {
   203	                log.WithContext(ctx).Error(err)
   204	        }
   205	
   206	        // enable single account mode only if configured by user and number of existing accounts is not grater than 1
   207	        am.singleAccountMode = singleAccountModeDomain != "" && accountsCounter <= 1
   208	        if am.singleAccountMode {
   209	                if !isDomainValid(singleAccountModeDomain) {
   210	                        return nil, status.Errorf(status.InvalidArgument, "invalid domain \"%s\" provided for a single account mode. Please review your input for --single-account-mode-domain", singleAccountModeDomain)
   211	                }
   212	                am.singleAccountModeDomain = singleAccountModeDomain
   213	                log.WithContext(ctx).Infof("single account mode enabled, accounts number %d", accountsCounter)
   214	        } else {
   215	                log.WithContext(ctx).Infof("single account mode disabled, accounts number %d", accountsCounter)
   216	        }
   217	
   218	        cacheStore, err := nbcache.NewStore(ctx, nbcache.DefaultIDPCacheExpirationMax, nbcache.DefaultIDPCacheCleanupInterval)
   219	        if err != nil {
   220	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("getting cache store: %s", err)
   221	        }
   222	        am.externalCacheManager = nbcache.NewUserDataCache(cacheStore)
   223	        am.cacheManager = nbcache.NewAccountUserDataCache(am.loadAccount, cacheStore)
   224	
   225	        if !isNil(am.idpManager) {
   226	                go func() {
   227	                        err := am.warmupIDPCache(ctx, cacheStore)
   228	                        if err != nil {
   229	                                log.WithContext(ctx).Warnf("failed warming up cache due to error: %v", err)
   230	                                // todo retry?
   231	                                return
   232	                        }
   233	                }()
   234	        }
   235	
   236	        am.integratedPeerValidator.SetPeerInvalidationListener(func(accountID string) {
   237	                am.onPeersInvalidated(ctx, accountID)
   238	        })
   239	
   240	        return am, nil
   241	}

   784	// GetOrCreateAccountByUser returns an existing account for a given user id or creates a new one if doesn't exist
   785	func (am *DefaultAccountManager) GetOrCreateAccountByUser(ctx context.Context, userID, domain string) (*types.Account, error) {
   786	        start := time.Now()
   787	        unlock := am.Store.AcquireGlobalLock(ctx)
   788	        defer unlock()
   789	        log.WithContext(ctx).Debugf("Acquired global lock in %s for user %s", time.Since(start), userID)
   790	
   791	        lowerDomain := strings.ToLower(domain)
   792	
   793	        account, err := am.Store.GetAccountByUser(ctx, userID)
   794	        if err != nil {
   795	                if s, ok := status.FromError(err); ok && s.Type() == status.NotFound {
   796	                        account, err = am.newAccount(ctx, userID, lowerDomain)
   797	                        if err != nil {
   798	                                return nil, err
   799	                        }
   800	                        err = am.Store.SaveAccount(ctx, account)
   801	                        if err != nil {
   802	                                return nil, err
   803	                        }
   804	                } else {
   805	                        // other error
   806	                        return nil, err
   807	                }
   808	        }
   809	
   810	        userObj := account.Users[userID]
   811	
   812	        if lowerDomain != "" && account.Domain != lowerDomain && userObj.Role == types.UserRoleOwner {
   813	                account.Domain = lowerDomain
   814	                err = am.Store.SaveAccount(ctx, account)
   815	                if err != nil {
   816	                        return nil, status.Errorf(status.Internal, "failed updating account with domain")
   817	                }
   818	        }
   819	
   820	        return account, nil
   821	}
   822	
   823	// GetUsersFromAccount performs a batched request for users from IDP by account ID apply filter on what data to return
   824	// based on provided user role.
   825	func (am *DefaultAccountManager) GetUsersFromAccount(ctx context.Context, accountID, initiatorUserID string) (map[string]*types.UserInfo, error) {
   826	        allowed, err := am.permissionsManager.ValidateUserPermissions(ctx, accountID, initiatorUserID, modules.Users, operations.Read)
   827	        if err != nil {
   828	                return nil, status.NewPermissionValidationError(err)
   829	        }
   830	
   831	        var user *types.User
   832	        if initiatorUserID != activity.SystemInitiator {
   833	                result, err := am.Store.GetUserByUserID(ctx, store.LockingStrengthShare, initiatorUserID)
   834	                if err != nil {
   835	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get user: %w", err)
   836	                }
   837	                user = result
   838	        }
   839	
   840	        accountUsers := []*types.User{}
   841	        switch {
   842	        case allowed:
   843	                accountUsers, err = am.Store.GetAccountUsers(ctx, store.LockingStrengthShare, accountID)
   844	                if err != nil {
   845	                        return nil, err
   846	                }
   847	        case user != nil && user.AccountID == accountID:
   848	                accountUsers = append(accountUsers, user)
   849	        default:
   850	                return map[string]*types.UserInfo{}, nil

   523	
   524	// newAccount creates a new Account with a generated ID and generated default setup keys.
   525	// If ID is already in use (due to collision) we try one more time before returning error
   526	func (am *DefaultAccountManager) newAccount(ctx context.Context, userID, domain string) (*types.Account, error) {
   527	        for i := 0; i < 2; i++ {
   528	                accountId := xid.New().String()
   529	
   530	                _, err := am.Store.GetAccount(ctx, accountId)
   531	                statusErr, _ := status.FromError(err)
   532	                switch {
   533	                case err == nil:
   534	                        log.WithContext(ctx).Warnf("an account with ID already exists, retrying...")
   535	                        continue
   536	                case statusErr.Type() == status.NotFound:
   537	                        newAccount := newAccountWithId(ctx, accountId, userID, domain)
   538	                        am.StoreEvent(ctx, userID, newAccount.Id, accountId, activity.AccountCreated, nil)
   539	                        return newAccount, nil
   540	                default:
   541	                        return nil, err
   542	                }
   543	        }
   544	
   545	        return nil, status.Errorf(status.Internal, "error while creating new account")
   546	}
   547	
   548	func (am *DefaultAccountManager) warmupIDPCache(ctx context.Context, store cacheStore.StoreInterface) error {
   549	        cold, err := am.isCacheCold(ctx, store)
   550	        if err != nil {
   551	                return err
   552	        }
   553	
   554	        if !cold {
   555	                log.WithContext(ctx).Debug("cache already populated, skipping warm up")
   556	                return nil
   557	        }
   558	
   559	        if delayStr, ok := os.LookupEnv("NB_IDP_CACHE_WARMUP_DELAY"); ok {
   560	                delay, err := time.ParseDuration(delayStr)
   561	                if err != nil {
   562	                        return fmt.Errorf("invalid IDP warmup delay: %w", err)
   563	                }
   564	                time.Sleep(delay)
   565	        }
   566	
   567	        userData, err := am.idpManager.GetAllAccounts(ctx)
   568	        if err != nil {
   569	                return err
   570	        }
   571	        log.WithContext(ctx).Infof("%d entries received from IdP management", len(userData))
   572	
   573	        // If the Identity Provider does not support writing AppMetadata,
   574	        // in cases like this, we expect it to return all users in an "unset" field.
   575	        // We iterate over the users in the "unset" field, look up their AccountID in our store, and
   576	        // update their AppMetadata with the AccountID.
   577	        if unsetData, ok := userData[idp.UnsetAccountID]; ok {
   578	                for _, user := range unsetData {
   579	                        accountID, err := am.Store.GetAccountByUser(ctx, user.ID)
   580	                        if err == nil {

  1731	// separateGroups separates user's auto groups into non-JWT and JWT groups.
  1732	// Returns the list of standard auto groups and a map of JWT auto groups,
  1733	// where the keys are the group names and the values are the group IDs.
  1734	func separateGroups(autoGroups []string, allGroups []*types.Group) ([]string, map[string]string) {
  1735	        newAutoGroups := make([]string, 0)
  1736	        jwtAutoGroups := make(map[string]string) // map of group name to group ID
  1737	
  1738	        allGroupsMap := make(map[string]*types.Group, len(allGroups))
  1739	        for _, group := range allGroups {
  1740	                allGroupsMap[group.ID] = group
  1741	        }
  1742	
  1743	        for _, id := range autoGroups {
  1744	                if group, ok := allGroupsMap[id]; ok {
  1745	                        if group.Issued == types.GroupIssuedJWT {
  1746	                                jwtAutoGroups[group.Name] = id
  1747	                        } else {
  1748	                                newAutoGroups = append(newAutoGroups, id)
  1749	                        }
  1750	                }

    58	// GetAuthAudiences returns the audience from the http config and device authorization flow config
    59	func (c Config) GetAuthAudiences() []string {
    60	        audiences := []string{c.HttpConfig.AuthAudience}
    61	
    62	        if c.HttpConfig.ExtraAuthAudience != "" {
    63	                audiences = append(audiences, c.HttpConfig.ExtraAuthAudience)
    64	        }
    65	
    66	        if c.DeviceAuthorizationFlow != nil && c.DeviceAuthorizationFlow.ProviderConfig.Audience != "" {
    67	                audiences = append(audiences, c.DeviceAuthorizationFlow.ProviderConfig.Audience)
    68	        }
    69	
    70	        return audiences
    71	}

OBSERVATION:

package types

import (
        "time"
)

// Settings represents Account settings structure that can be modified via API and Dashboard
type Settings struct {
        // PeerLoginExpirationEnabled globally enables or disables peer login expiration
        PeerLoginExpirationEnabled bool

        // PeerLoginExpiration is a setting that indicates when peer login expires.
        // Applies to all peers that have Peer.LoginExpirationEnabled set to true.
        PeerLoginExpiration time.Duration

        // PeerInactivityExpirationEnabled globally enables or disables peer inactivity expiration
        PeerInactivityExpirationEnabled bool

        // PeerInactivityExpiration is a setting that indicates when peer inactivity expires.
        // Applies to all peers that have Peer.PeerInactivityExpirationEnabled set to true.
        PeerInactivityExpiration time.Duration

        // RegularUsersViewBlocked allows to block regular users from viewing even their own peers and some UI elements
        RegularUsersViewBlocked bool

        // GroupsPropagationEnabled allows to propagate auto groups from the user to the peer
        GroupsPropagationEnabled bool

        // JWTGroupsEnabled allows extract groups from JWT claim, which name defined in the JWTGroupsClaimName
        // and add it to account groups.
        JWTGroupsEnabled bool

        // JWTGroupsClaimName from which we extract groups name to add it to account groups
        JWTGroupsClaimName string

        // JWTAllowGroups list of groups to which users are allowed access
        JWTAllowGroups []string `gorm:"serializer:json"`

        // RoutingPeerDNSResolutionEnabled enabled the DNS resolution on the routing peers
        RoutingPeerDNSResolutionEnabled bool

        // DNSDomain is the custom domain for that account
        DNSDomain string

        // Extra is a dictionary of Account settings
        Extra *ExtraSettings `gorm:"embedded;embeddedPrefix:extra_"`

        // LazyConnectionEnabled indicates if the experimental feature is enabled or disabled
        LazyConnectionEnabled bool `gorm:"default:false"`
}
        // DisableAutoPolicy globally disables the creation of the default all-to-all policy
        DisableAutoPolicy bool `gorm:"default:false"`

// Copy copies the Settings struct
func (s *Settings) Copy() *Settings {
        settings := &Settings{
                PeerLoginExpirationEnabled: s.PeerLoginExpirationEnabled,
                PeerLoginExpiration:        s.PeerLoginExpiration,
                JWTGroupsEnabled:           s.JWTGroupsEnabled,
                JWTGroupsClaimName:         s.JWTGroupsClaimName,

package types

import (
        "time"
)

// Settings represents Account settings structure that can be modified via API and Dashboard
type Settings struct {
        // PeerLoginExpirationEnabled globally enables or disables peer login expiration
        PeerLoginExpirationEnabled bool

        // PeerLoginExpiration is a setting that indicates when peer login expires.
        // Applies to all peers that have Peer.LoginExpirationEnabled set to true.
        PeerLoginExpiration time.Duration

        // PeerInactivityExpirationEnabled globally enables or disables peer inactivity expiration
        PeerInactivityExpirationEnabled bool

        // PeerInactivityExpiration is a setting that indicates when peer inactivity expires.
        // Applies to all peers that have Peer.PeerInactivityExpirationEnabled set to true.
        PeerInactivityExpiration time.Duration

        // RegularUsersViewBlocked allows to block regular users from viewing even their own peers and some UI elements
        RegularUsersViewBlocked bool

        // GroupsPropagationEnabled allows to propagate auto groups from the user to the peer
        GroupsPropagationEnabled bool

        // JWTGroupsEnabled allows extract groups from JWT claim, which name defined in the JWTGroupsClaimName
        // and add it to account groups.
        JWTGroupsEnabled bool

        // JWTGroupsClaimName from which we extract groups name to add it to account groups
        JWTGroupsClaimName string

        // JWTAllowGroups list of groups to which users are allowed access
        JWTAllowGroups []string `gorm:"serializer:json"`

        // RoutingPeerDNSResolutionEnabled enabled the DNS resolution on the routing peers
        RoutingPeerDNSResolutionEnabled bool

        // DNSDomain is the custom domain for that account
        DNSDomain string

        // Extra is a dictionary of Account settings
        Extra *ExtraSettings `gorm:"embedded;embeddedPrefix:extra_"`

        // LazyConnectionEnabled indicates if the experimental feature is enabled or disabled
LazyConnectionEnabled bool `gorm:"default:false"`

	// DisableAutoPolicy globally disables the creation of the default all-to-all policy
	DisableAutoPolicy bool `gorm:"default:false"`
}
// Copy copies the Settings struct
func (s *Settings) Copy() *Settings {
        settings := &Settings{
                PeerLoginExpirationEnabled: s.PeerLoginExpirationEnabled,
                PeerLoginExpiration:        s.PeerLoginExpiration,
                JWTGroupsEnabled:           s.JWTGroupsEnabled,
                JWTGroupsClaimName:         s.JWTGroupsClaimName,
                GroupsPropagationEnabled:   s.GroupsPropagationEnabled,
                JWTAllowGroups:             s.JWTAllowGroups,
                RegularUsersViewBlocked:    s.RegularUsersViewBlocked,

                PeerInactivityExpirationEnabled: s.PeerInactivityExpirationEnabled,
                PeerInactivityExpiration:        s.PeerInactivityExpiration,

                RoutingPeerDNSResolutionEnabled: s.RoutingPeerDNSResolutionEnabled,
                LazyConnectionEnabled:           s.LazyConnectionEnabled,
                DNSDomain:                       s.DNSDomain,
                DisableAutoPolicy:               s.DisableAutoPolicy,
        }
        if s.Extra != nil {
                settings.Extra = s.Extra.Copy()
        }
        return settings
}

type ExtraSettings struct {
        // PeerApprovalEnabled enables or disables the need for peers bo be approved by an administrator
        PeerApprovalEnabled bool

        // IntegratedValidatorGroups list of group IDs to be used with integrated approval configurations
        IntegratedValidatorGroups []string `gorm:"serializer:json"`

        FlowEnabled              bool `gorm:"-"`
        FlowPacketCounterEnabled bool `gorm:"-"`
        FlowENCollectionEnabled  bool `gorm:"-"`
        FlowDnsCollectionEnabled bool `gorm:"-"`
}

// Copy copies the ExtraSettings struct
func (e *ExtraSettings) Copy() *ExtraSettings {
        var cpGroup []string

        return &ExtraSettings{
                PeerApprovalEnabled:       e.PeerApprovalEnabled,
                IntegratedValidatorGroups: append(cpGroup, e.IntegratedValidatorGroups...),
        }
}
